36:["$","h2",null,{"children":"feature() and Bun Compile-Time Dead Code Elimination"}]
37:["$","p",null,{"children":["Claude Code uses Bun for building and bundling. Bun provides a special module ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"bun:bundle"}]," whose ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," function implements compile-time conditional compilation — this is not a runtime feature flag but a decision made at build time about whether code is included in the final output."]}]
39:["$","h3",null,{"children":"How It Works"}]
3a:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," is evaluated at compile time to a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"true"}]," or ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"false"}]," constant. Bun's bundler (or the JavaScript engine's dead code elimination) then removes branches that will never execute. This means disabled features don't just avoid execution — their ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"entire module trees"}]," are never loaded."]}]
3b:["$","p",null,{"children":["In ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"src/commands.ts"}],", this pattern is used extensively:"]}]
3d:["$","p",null,{"children":["Note the use of ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," rather than ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"import"}]," — this is intentional. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"import"}]," is static and will be executed during module evaluation regardless of any surrounding conditions. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," is dynamic and only executes when ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," returns ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"true"}],". When ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," evaluates to ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"false"}]," at compile time, the entire ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," call (and its dependency tree) is eliminated."]}]

6e:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Deferred Require Pattern for Circular Dependencies"}]
6f:["$","p",null,{"children":["In a large project with 1,900+ files, circular dependencies are nearly unavoidable. Claude Code uses deferred ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," functions to break cycles:"]}]
71:["$","p",null,{"children":["The same pattern appears in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"main.tsx"}],":"]}]
73:["$","p",null,{"children":"This pattern has several clever aspects:"}]
74:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Function wrapping"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"const getX = () => require('...')"}]," ensures ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," is only executed when the function is called, not during module evaluation"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Type safety"}],": ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"as typeof import('...')"}]," preserves full TypeScript type inference"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Caching"}],": Node.js/Bun's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," has built-in module caching, so calling ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"getTeamCreateTool()"}]," multiple times only loads the module once"]}],"\n"]}]
75:["$","p",null,{"children":["The difference from the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," pattern is: ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," is a compile-time decision — code either exists or doesn't; deferred ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," is a runtime strategy — code always exists in the bundle but loading is postponed until first use."]}]

81:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Deferred Evaluation and Memoization of Command Lists"}]
82:["$","p",null,{"children":"Command list construction embodies the same philosophy — declared as a function to defer evaluation until first invocation:"}]
84:["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"memoize()"}]," ensures the command list is built only once. 85:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Session Restoration Paths: teleport, remote, resume"}]

8f:["$","h3",null,{"children":"--teleport: Cross-Device Restoration"}]

94:["$","h3",null,{"children":"Interaction Between Restoration Paths and Startup Hooks"}]
95:["$","p",null,{"children":"A subtle but important detail: restoration paths skip startup hooks:"}]
97:["$","p",null,{"children":["This is because when restoring a session, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"conversationRecovery.ts"}]," triggers a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"'resume'"}]," type hook, avoiding duplicate execution with the startup hook."]}]
98:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Parallelizing setup() and Command Loading"}]
99:["$","p",null,{"children":["In the action handler, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"setup()"}]," and command/agent loading are parallelized:"]}]
9b:["$","p",null,{"children":"Several design decisions are worth noting:"}]
9c:["$","ol",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":["\n",["$","p",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"initBuiltinPlugins()"}]," and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"initBundledSkills()"}]," execute synchronously before parallel launches — they are pure in-memory operations (<1ms, zero I/O), but ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"getCommands()"}]," internally calls ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"getBundledSkills()"}]," which synchronously reads their results. 9d:["$","h2",null,{"children":"Transferable Patterns: Cold Start Optimization Checklist for Large CLIs"}]
9e:["$","p",null,{"children":"From Claude Code's startup optimization, we can distill a general-purpose cold start optimization checklist for large CLIs:"}]
9f:["$","h3",null,{"children":"1. Phased Initialization + Checkpoint Marking"}]
a0:["$","p",null,{"children":"Split the startup process into distinct phases, mark each with checkpoints, and establish a quantifiable performance baseline:"}]
a2:["$","p",null,{"children":["Don't guess where it's slow — use data. Claude Code's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"profileCheckpoint()"}]," system has zero overhead for 99.5% of cases, collecting data only from sampled users."]}]
a3:["$","h3",null,{"children":"2. \"Fire Early, Collect Late\" Parallel I/O"}]
a4:["$","p",null,{"children":"Identify I/O operations in the startup path (file reads, subprocess calls, network requests), launch them at the earliest possible moment, and collect results at the latest moment they're needed:"}]
a6:["$","h3",null,{"children":"3. Compile-Time Elimination > Runtime Checks"}]
a7:["$","p",null,{"children":["If you know a feature won't be used in a particular build configuration, eliminate it at compile time rather than skipping it at runtime. Bun's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"feature()"}]," is one implementation; Webpack's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"DefinePlugin"}]," + ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"NormalModuleReplacementPlugin"}]," is another. The key is enabling the bundler's tree-shaking to remove entire unused module trees."]}]
a8:["$","h3",null,{"children":"4. Lazy Shim Pattern"}]
a9:["$","p",null,{"children":"For components that need metadata at registration time but full code only at execution time (commands, routes, plugins), create lightweight shim objects:"}]
ab:["$","h3",null,{"children":"5. Deferred Require to Break Circular Dependencies"}]
ac:["$","p",null,{"children":["In large codebases, fully resolving circular dependencies through refactoring is often prohibitively expensive. Function-wrapped ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"require()"}]," breaks cycles with minimal invasiveness while maintaining type safety:"]}]
ae:["$","h3",null,{"children":"6. Mode-Aware Fast Paths"}]
af:["$","p",null,{"children":["Skip unnecessary initialization based on the running mode. Claude Code skips registration of 52 subcommands in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"-p/--print"}]," mode (saving 65ms) and skips hooks, LSP, plugins, and all non-essential components in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"--bare"}]," mode:"]}]
b1:["$","h3",null,{"children":"7. Memoize Expensive Computations"}]
b2:["$","p",null,{"children":["Once command lists, tool lists, and skill lists are computed, cache results via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"lodash/memoize"}],":"]}]
b4:["$","p",null,{"children":["When caches need invalidation (e.g., a new skill was dynamically added), provide an explicit ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"clearCache()"}]," method:"]}]
b6:["$","h3",null,{"children":"8. Minimize Import Chains"}]
b7:["$","p",null,{"children":["Prefetch modules (like ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"keychainPrefetch.ts"}],") must maintain minimal import chains. If the prefetch module itself pulls in heavy dependencies, the parallel advantage of prefetching is negated by the synchronous module evaluation overhead. Clearly comment why you chose ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"child_process"}]," over ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"execa"}],", and why you import ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"helpers"}]," rather than ",["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"storage"}],"."]}]
b8:["$","h3",null,{"children":"9. Non-Blocking Background Tasks"}]
b9:["$","p",null,{"children":"Place cleanup, syncing, prefetching, and other non-critical tasks in the background:"}]
bb:["$","h3",null,{"children":"10. Observability First"}]
bc:["$","p",null,{"children":"Before optimizing, establish observability. Claude Code's approach:"}]
bd:["$","ul",null,{"children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Sampled reporting to Statsig (production monitoring)"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"rounded bg-[#1a1a2e] px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[0.875em] text-[#e0c4a8] before:content-none after:content-none","children":"CLAUDE_CODE_PROFILE_STARTUP=1"}]," detailed reports (local debugging)"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Duration and memory usage for each phase"}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"children":"Automatic detection and reporting of performance regressions"}],"\n"]}]
be:["$","p",null,{"children":"Without measurement, there is no optimization. Without continuous monitoring, optimizations degrade as new features are added."}]

c0:["$","p",null,{"children":"Claude Code's cold start optimization isn't a single silver bullet but a combination of carefully designed techniques:"}]
